compactable blocks in the provided directory.\\n222: func (c *LeveledCompactor) Plan(dir string) ([]string, error) {\\n223: \\tdirs, err := blockDirs(dir)\\n224: \\tif err != nil {\\n225: \\t\\treturn \\n254: \\tres := c.selectOverlappingDirs(dms)\\n255: \\tif len(res) > 0 {\\n256: \\t\\treturn res, nil\\n257: \\t}\\n258: \\t// No overlapping blocks, do compaction the usual way.\\n259: \\t// We do having to care about data overlap.\\n261: \\tdms = dms[:len(dms)-1]\\n262: \\n263: \\tfor _, dm := range c.selectDirs(dms) {\\n264: \\t\\tres = append(res, dm.dir)\\n265: \\t}\\n266: \\tif len(res) > \\n289: // selectDirs returns the dir metas that should be compacted into a single new block.\\n290: // If only a single block range is configured, the result is always nil.\\n291: func (c *LeveledCompactor) selectDirs(ds []dirMeta) []dirMeta {\\n292: \\tif len(c.ranges) < 2 || len(ds) < 1 {\\n293: \\t\\treturn nil\\n294: \\t}\\n295: \\n296: \\thighTime := ds[len(ds)-1].meta.MinTime\\n297: \\n298: \\tfor _, iv := range c.ranges[1:] {\\n299: \\t\\tparts := splitByRange(ds, iv)\\n300: \\t\\tif len(parts) == 0 {\\n301: \\t\\t\\tcontinue\\n302: \\t\\t}\\n303: \\n304: \\tOuter:\\n305: \\t\\tfor _, p := range parts {\\n306: \\t\\t\\t// Do not select the range if it has a block whose compaction failed.\\n307: \\t\\t\\tfor _, dm := range p {\\n308: \\t\\t\\t\\tif dm.meta.Compaction.Failed {\\n309: \\t\\t\\t\\t\\tcontinue Outer\\n310: \\t\\t\\t\\t}\\n311: \\t\\t\\t}\\n312: \\n313: \\t\\t\\tmint := p[0].meta.MinTime\\n314: \\t\\t\\tmaxt := p[len(p)-1].meta.MaxTime\\n315: \\t\\t\\t// Pick the range of blocks if it spans the full range (potentially with gaps)\\n316: \\t\\t\\t// or is before the most recent block.\\n317: \\t\\t\\t// This ensures we don't compact blocks prematurely when another one of the same\\n318: \\t\\t\\t// size still fits in the range.\\n319: \\t\\t\\tif (maxt-mint == iv || maxt <= highTime) && len(p) > 1 {\\n320: \\t\\t\\t\\treturn p\\n321: \\t\\t\\t}\\n322: \\t\\t}\\n323: \\t}\\n324: \\n325: \\treturn nil\\n326: }\\n327: \\n328: // selectOverlappingDirs returns all dirs with overlapping time ranges.\\n329: // It expects sorted input by mint and returns the overlapping dirs in the same order as received.\\n330: func (c *LeveledCompactor) selectOverlappingDirs(ds []dirMeta) []string {\\n331: \\tif !c.enableOverlappingCompaction {\\n332: \\t\\treturn nil\\n333: \\t}\\n334: \\tif len(ds) < 2 {\\n335: \\t\\treturn nil\\n336: \\t}\\n337: \\tvar overlappingDirs []string\\n338: \\tglobalMaxt := ds[0].meta.MaxTime\\n339: \\tfor i, d := range ds[1:] {\\n340: \\t\\tif d.meta.MinTime < globalMaxt {\\n341: \\t\\t\\tif len(overlappingDirs) == 0 { // When it is the first overlap, need to add the last one as well.\\n342: \\t\\t\\t\\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, ds[i].dir)\\n343: \\t\\t\\t}\\n344: \\t\\t\\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, d.dir)\\n345: \\t\\t} else if len(overlappingDirs) > 0 {\\n346: \\t\\t\\tbreak\\n347: \\t\\t}\\n348: \\t\\tif d.meta.MaxTime > globalMaxt {\\n349: \\t\\t\\tglobalMaxt = d.meta.MaxTime\\n350: \\t\\t}\\n351: \\t}\\n352: \\treturn overlappingDirs\\n353: }\\n354: \\n355: // splitByRange splits the directories by the time range. The range sequence starts at 0.\\n356: //\\n357: // For example, if we have blocks [0-10, 10-20, 50-60, 90-100] and the split range tr is 30\\n358: // it returns [0-10, 10-20], [50-60], [90-100].\\n359: func splitByRange(ds []dirMeta, tr int64) [][]dirMeta {\\n360: \\tvar splitDirs [][]dirMeta\\n361: \\n362: \\tfor i := 0; i < len(ds); {\\n363: \\t\\tvar (\\n364: \\t\\t\\tgroup []dirMeta\\n365: \\t\\t\\tt0    int64\\n366: \\t\\t\\tm     = ds[i].meta\\n367: \\t\\t)\\n368: \\t\\t// Compute start of aligned time range of size tr closest to the current block's start.\\n369: \\t\\tif m.MinTime >= 0 {\\n370: \\t\\t\\tt0 = tr * (m.MinTime / tr)\\n371: \\t\\t} else {\\n372: \\t\\t\\tt0 = tr * ((m.MinTime - tr + 1) / tr)\\n373: \\t\\t}\\n374: \\t\\t// Skip blocks that don't fall into the range. This can happen via mis-alignment or\\n375: \\t\\t// by being the multiple of the intended range.\\n376: \\t\\tif m.MaxTime > t0+tr {\\n377: \\t\\t\\ti++\\n378: \\t\\t\\tcontinue\\n379: \\t\\t}\\n380: \\n381: \\t\\t// Add all dirs to the current group that are within [t0, t0+tr].\\n382: \\t\\tfor ; i < len(ds); i++ {\\n383: \\t\\t\\t// Either the block falls into the next range or doesn't fit at all (checked above).\\n384: \\t\\t\\tif ds[i].meta.MaxTime > t0+tr {\\n385: \\t\\t\\t\\tbreak\\n386: \\t\\t\\t}\\n387: \\t\\t\\tgroup = append(group, ds[i])\\n388: \\t\\t}\\n389: \\n390: \\t\\tif len(group) > 0 {\\n391: \\t\\t\\tsplitDirs = append(splitDirs, group)\\n392: \\t\\t}\\n393: \\t}\\n394: \\n395: \\treturn splitDirs\\n396: }\\n397: \\n398: // CompactBlockMetas merges many block metas into one, combining it's source blocks together\\n399: // and adjusting compaction level. single tombstone is for distinct series, which might be no true.\n276: \t\t\tif meta.Stats.NumTombstones > 0 && meta.Stats.NumTombstones >= meta.Stats.NumSeries {\n277: \t\t\t\treturn []string{dms[i].dir}, nil\n278: \t\t\t}\n279: \t\t\tbreak\n280: \t\t}\n281: \t\tif float64(meta.Stats.NumTombstones)/float64(meta.Stats.NumSeries+1) > 0.05 {\n282: \t\t\treturn []string{dms[i].dir}, nil\n283: \t\t}\n284: \t}\n285: \n286: \treturn nil, nil\n287: }\n288: \n289: // selectDirs returns the dir metas that should be compacted into a single new block.\n290: // If only a single block range is configured, the result is always nil.\n291: func (c *LeveledCompactor) selectDirs(ds []dirMeta) []dirMeta {\n292: \tif len(c.ranges) < 2 || len(ds) < 1 {\n293: \t\treturn nil\n294: \t}\n295: \n296: \thighTime := ds[len(ds)-1].meta.MinTime\n297: \n298: \tfor _, iv := range c.ranges[1:] {\n299: \t\tparts := splitByRange(ds, iv)\n300: \t\tif len(parts) == 0 {\n301: \t\t\tcontinue\n302: \t\t}\n303: \n304: \tOuter:\n305: \t\tfor _, p := range parts {\n306: \t\t\t// Do not select the range if it has a block whose compaction failed.\n307: \t\t\tfor _, dm := range p {\n308: \t\t\t\tif \n325: \treturn nil\n326: }\n327: \n328: // selectOverlappingDirs returns all dirs with overlapping time ranges.\n329: // It expects sorted input by mint and returns the overlapping dirs in the same order as received.\n330: func (c *LeveledCompactor) selectOverlappingDirs(ds []dirMeta) []string {\n331: \tif !c.enableOverlappingCompaction {\n332: \t\treturn nil\n333: \t}\n334: \tif len(ds) < 2 The range sequence starts at 0.\n356: //\n357: // For example, if we have blocks [0-10, 10-20, 50-60, 90-100] and the split range tr is 30\n358: // it returns [0-10, 10-20], [50-60], [90-100].\n359: func splitByRange(ds []dirMeta, tr int64) [][]dirMeta {\n360: \tvar splitDirs [][]dirMeta\n361: \n362: \tfor i := 0; i < len(ds); {\n363: \t\tvar (\n364: \t\t\tgroup []dirMeta\n365: \t\t\tt0    int64\n366: \t\t\tm     = ds[i].meta\n367: \t\t)\n368: \t\t// Compute start of aligned time range of size tr closest to the current block's start.\n369: \t\tif m.MinTime >= 0 {\n370: \t\t\tt0 = tr * (m.MinTime / tr)\n371: \t\t} else {\n372: \t\t\tt0 = tr * ((m.MinTime - tr + 1) / tr)\n373: \t\t}\n374: \t\t// Skip blocks that don't fall into the range. This can happen via mis-alignment or\n375: \t\t// by being the multiple of the intended range.\n376: \t\tif m.MaxTime > t0+tr {\n377: \t\t\ti++\n378: \t\t\tcontinue\n379: \t\t}\n380: \n381: \t\t// Add all dirs to the current group that are within [t0, t0+tr].\n382: \t\tfor ; i < len(ds); i++ {\n383: \t\t\t// Either the block falls into the next range or doesn't fit at all (checked above).\n384: \t\t\tif ds[i].meta.MaxTime > t0+tr {\n385: \t\t\t\tbreak\n386: \t\t\t}\n387: \t\t\tgroup = append(group, ds[i])\n388: \t\t}\n389: \n390: \t\tif len(group) > 0 {\n391: \t\t\tsplitDirs = append(splitDirs, group)\n392: \t\t}\n393: \t}\n394: \n395: \treturn splitDirs\n396: }\n397: \n398: // CompactBlockMetas merges many block metas into one, combining it's source blocks together\n399: // and adjusting compaction level. Min/Max time of result block meta covers all input blocks.\n400: func CompactBlockMetas(uid ulid.ULID, blocks ...*BlockMeta) *BlockMeta {\n401: \tres := &BlockMeta{\n402: \t\tULID: uid,\n403: \t\treturn a.Compare(b)\n435: \t})\n436: \n437: \tres.MinTime = mint\n438: \tres.MaxTime = maxt\n439: \treturn res\n440: }\n441: \n442: // Compact creates a new block in the compactor's directory from But\n1171: \t\t// chunk intervals are closed: [c.MinTime, c.MaxTime];\n1172: \t\t// so in order to make sure that overlaps are evaluated\n1173: \t\t// consistently, we explicitly remove the last value\n1174: \t\t// from the block interval here.\n1175: \t\trh := NewRangeHeadWithIsolationDisabled(db.head, mint, maxt-1)\n1176: \n1177: \t\t// Compaction runs with isolation disabled, because head.compactable()\n1178: \t\t// ensures that maxt is more than chunkRange/2 back from now, and\n1179: \t\t// head.appendableMinValidTime() ensures that no new appends can start within the compaction range.\n1180: \t\t// We do need to wait for any overlapping appenders that started previously to finish.\n1181: \t\tdb.head.WaitForAppendersOverlapping(rh.MaxTime())\n1182: \n1183: \t\tif err := db.compactHead(rh); err != nil {\n1184: \t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"compact head: %w\", err)\n1185: \t\t}\n1186: \t\t// Consider only successful compactions for WAL truncation.\n1187: \t\tlastBlockMaxt = maxt\n1188: \t}\n1189: \n1190: \t// Clear some disk space before compacting blocks, especially important\n1191: \t// when Head compaction happened over a long time range.\n1192: \tif err := db.head.truncateWAL(lastBlockMaxt); err != nil {\n1193: \t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"WAL truncation in Compact: %w\", err)\n1194: \t}\n1195: \n1196: \tcompactionDuration := time.Since(start)\n1197: \tif compactionDuration.Milliseconds() > db.head.chunkRange.Load() {\n1198: \t\tlevel.Warn(db.logger).Log(\n1199: \t\t\t\"msg\", \"Head compaction took longer than the block time range, compactions are falling behind and won't be able to catch up\",\n1200: \t\t\t\"duration\", compactionDuration.String(),\n1201: ","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/prometheus--v2.52.0@c4ebcdb2ffc708e664ce8642ce6f84730335c34e/-/blob/tsdb/db.go%3FL1000-1200"}}}

For a given posting, its shard MUST be computed hashing\\n86: \\t// the series labels mod shardCount, using a hash function which is consistent over time.\\n87: \\tShardedPostings(p index.Postings, shardIndex, shardCount uint64) index.Postings\\n88: \\n89: \\t// Series populates the given builder and chunk metas for the series identified\\n90: \\t// by the reference.\\n91: \\t// Returns storage.ErrNotFound if the ref does not resolve to a known series.\\n92: \\tSeries(ref storage.SeriesRef, builder *labels.ScratchBuilder, chks *[]chunks.Meta) error\\n93: \\n94: \\t// LabelNames returns all the unique label names present in the index in sorted order.\\n95: \\tLabelNames(ctx context.Context, matchers ...*labels.Matcher) ([]string, error)\\n96: \\n97: \\t// LabelValueFor returns label value for the given label name in the series referred to by ID.\\n98: \\t// If the series couldn't be found or the series doesn't have the requested label a\\n99: \\t// storage.ErrNotFound is returned as error.\\n100: \\tLabelValueFor(ctx context.Context, id storage.SeriesRef, label string) (string, error)\\n101: \\n102: \\t// LabelNamesFor returns all the label names for the series referred to by IDs.\\n103: \\t// The names returned are sorted.\\n104: \\tLabelNamesFor(ctx context.Context, ids ...storage.SeriesRef) ([]string, error)\\n105: \\n106: \\t// Close releases the underlying resources of the reader.\\n107: \\tClose() error\\n108: }\\n109: \\n110: // ChunkWriter serializes a time block of chunked series data.\\n111: type ChunkWriter interface {\\n112: \\t// WriteChunks writes several chunks. The Chunk field of the ChunkMetas\\n113: \\t// must be populated.\\n114: \\t// After returning successfully, the Ref fields in the ChunkMetas\\n115: \\t// are set and can be used to retrieve the chunks from the written data.\\n116: \\tWriteChunks(chunks ...chunks.Meta) error\\n117: \\n118: \\t// Close writes any required finalization and closes the resources\\n119: \\t// associated with the underlying writer.\\n120: \\tClose() error\\n121: }\\n122: \\n123: // ChunkReader provides reading access of serialized time series data.\\n124: type ChunkReader interface {\\n125: \\t// ChunkOrIterable returns the series data for the given chunks.Meta.\\n126: \\t// Either a single chunk will be returned, or an iterable.\\n127: \\t// A single chunk should be returned if chunks.Meta maps to a chunk that\\n128: \\t// already exists and doesn't need modifications.\\n129: \\t// An iterable should be returned if chunks.Meta maps to a subset of the\\n130: \\t// samples in a stored chunk, or multiple chunks. (E.g. OOOHeadChunkReader\\n131: \\t// could return an iterable where multiple histogram samples have counter\\n132: \\t// resets. {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_0111G3LVKTM7YoPqHzwVmxJs","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01Q367A2yHFLHAUJGhbgnnsM","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/documentation.md","content":"# Prometheus TSDB Compaction Operational Runbook\n\n## 1. Overview\n\n### What Compaction Does\n\nCompaction in Prometheus TSDB merges multiple time-series data blocks into larger, more efficient blocks. This process:\n\n- **Merges overlapping blocks**: Combines blocks with overlapping time ranges into a single block to improve query performance and consistency\n- **Removes deleted series**: Eliminates tombstoned (deleted) series from blocks, reducing disk space usage\n- **Deduplicates samples**: Consolidates duplicate samples from overlapping blocks\n- **Optimizes index and chunk layout**: Reorganizes data for better I/O efficiency and memory locality\n\n### Compaction Levels and Block Structure\n\nPrometheus uses **exponential compaction levels**:\n\n- **Level 1**: Freshly persisted head blocks (2-hour default duration)\n- **Level 2**: First-level compaction (4-hour range)\n- **Level 3**: Second-level compaction (8-hour range)\n- **Level N**: Progressive doubling of time ranges\n\nEach level is defined by:\n- **MinTime (mint)**: Start timestamp (milliseconds, inclusive)\n- **MaxTime (maxt)**: End timestamp (milliseconds, exclusive)\n- **ULID**: Unique identifier for the block\n- **Compaction.Level**: Current compaction level\n- **Compaction.Parents**: Source blocks that were compacted\n- **Compaction.Sources**: Original blocks the compact traces back to\n\n### When Compaction is Triggered\n\nCompaction is triggered by three mechanisms:\n\n#### 1. Time-Based Triggering (Primary)\n- A background goroutine runs every **1 minute** (line 995 in db.go)\n- Checks if the head block is **compactable** (time window has passed)\n- Sends trigger signal to `compactc` channel\n\n#### 2. Appender-Based Triggering (On-Demand)\n- After each commit to the head block, checks `head.compactable()` (line 1120 in db.go)\n- If compactable, immediately triggers compaction without waiting for the 1-minute interval\n- Ensures fresh data is persisted promptly\n\n#### 3. Retention-Based Triggering (Post-Compaction)\n- After block compaction succeeds, `reloadBlocks()` checks for:\n  - **Time retention**: Blocks older than `RetentionDuration` are marked deletable\n  - **Size retention**: If `MaxBytes` is set, oldest blocks are removed until total size <= `MaxBytes`\n- Compaction plan considers blocks with **>5% tombstones** for cleanup (line 281 in compact.go)\n\n### Compaction Flow\n\n```\nHead Block Data (2h window)\n    ↓ (compactable after 1h min wait)\nHead Compaction → Level 1 Block\n    ↓ (time-based plan check)\nCompactor.Plan() → identifies compactable blocks\n    ↓\nCompactor.Compact() → merges blocks, removes tombstones\n    ↓\nDB.reloadBlocks() → swaps in new block, deletes parents\n    ↓\nRetention cleanup → removes old/oversized blocks\n```\n\n---\n\n## 2. Monitoring Indicators\n\n### Key Prometheus Metrics\n\n#### Compaction Activity Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Meaning | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|---------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` | Counter | Total compactions executed | Track for stalls (no increase for >10 min) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total` | Counter | Total compactions triggered | Should increase ~every 1 min |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` | Counter | Failed compactions | Alert if > 0 |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total` | Counter | Overlapping block compactions | Indicates overlapping blocks detected |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` | Histogram | Compaction wall-clock time | P95 > 5 min = slow compaction |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` | Gauge | 1 if block being written | Should be 0 for >30 sec (stuck write) |\n\n#### Block Management Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Meaning | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|---------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` | Gauge | Currently loaded blocks | Rapid increases = blocks not cleaning up |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes_total` | Gauge | Total block disk usage | Should trend toward `MaxBytes` limit |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_reloads_total` | Counter | Block reload operations | Once per minute (normal) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total` | Counter | Failed block reloads | Alert if > 0 |\n\n#### Chunk Compaction Metrics (Level 1 Only)\n\n| Metric | Type | Meaning | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|---------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_size_bytes` | Histogram | Final chunk sizes | Very small (<100 B) or large (>50 KB) chunks indicate compression issues |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_samples` | Histogram | Samples per chunk | <50 or >1000 samples per chunk = efficiency loss |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_range_seconds` | Histogram | Time span of chunks | Anomalies indicate data collection issues |\n\n### Alert Rules\n\n#### Critical Alerts (Act Immediately)\n\n```promql\n# Compaction is failing\nrate(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total[5m]) > 0\n\n# Block reload failures\nrate(prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total[5m]) > 0\n\n# Disk space about to be exhausted (if MaxBytes set)\nprometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes_total\n  / prometheus_tsdb_max_bytes_limit\n  > 0.95\n```\n\n#### Warning Alerts (Investigate Within 1 Hour)\n\n```promql\n# Compaction is stuck/slow\nrate(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total[10m]) == 0\n\n# Compaction taking too long\nhistogram_quantile(0.95,\n  prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds_bucket) > 300\n\n# Block populating stalled\nprometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block == 1\n  and time() - timestamp(prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block) > 30\n```\n\n### Healthy Compaction Patterns\n\n- **Compactions triggered**: ~1 per minute (every minute the goroutine checks)\n- **Compactions executed**: ~1 per 5-30 minutes (depends on block layout and activity)\n- **Compaction duration**: P50 < 1s, P99 < 5s (for typical setups)\n- **Blocks loaded**: Stable count (typically 10-50 for normal retention)\n- **Reload failures**: Zero\n- **Block bytes**: Trending toward configured limit\n\n---\n\n## 3. Failure Modes\n\n### Failure Mode 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n#### Symptoms\n- Compaction fails with \"no space left on device\" error\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` increases\n- New blocks cannot be persisted to disk\n- Ingestion slows or stops\n- In logs: `\"msg\":\"compact ... : no such file or directory\"` or similar I/O errors\n\n#### Root Causes\n1. **Retention duration too long**: `RetentionDuration` retains data beyond disk capacity\n2. **MaxBytes limit not enforced**: `MaxBytes` set but blocks not deleting fast enough\n3. **Compaction blocked**: Compaction unable to run → old blocks accumulate\n4. **Unexpected large metrics**: Cardinality explosion or high-frequency scraping\n5. **WAL growth**: Write-ahead log (WAL) consuming large disk space\n6. **Tmp block directories not cleaned**: Failed compactions leave `.tmp-for-creation` directories\n\n#### Diagnostic Steps\n\n1. **Check disk usage**:\n   ```bash\n   df -h /path/to/prometheus/data\n   du -sh /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb\n   du -sh /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/wal\n   ```\n\n2. **Inspect block count and size**:\n   ```bash\n   ls -lh /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/ | grep -E '^d' | wc -l\n   find /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb -name \"meta.json\" | wc -l\n   ```\n\n3. **Check for tmp directories**:\n   ```bash\n   find /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb -name \"*tmp*\" -type d\n   ```\n\n4. **Monitor compaction metrics**:\n   ```promql\n   rate(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total[5m])\n   prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes_total\n   ```\n\n5. **Check Prometheus logs for errors**:\n   ```bash\n   grep -i \"disk\\|space\\|compaction\\|failed\" /var/log/prometheus/*.log | tail -50\n   ```\n\n#### Code References\n- **Compaction triggering**: `tsdb/db.go:run()` (line 982-1027)\n- **Retention cleanup**: `tsdb/db.go:DefaultBlocksToDelete()` (defines retention policy)\n- **Compaction execution**: `tsdb/compact.go:LeveledCompactor.Compact()` (line 444)\n- **Disk space checks**: `tsdb/db.go:reloadBlocks()` (line 1424-1530)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 2: Compaction Stuck / Not Progressing\n\n#### Symptoms\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` metric flat (no increment for 10+ minutes)\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` gauge stuck at 1\n- Memory usage climbing or stable at high level\n- Queries slow (many blocks to search)\n- In logs: No \"msg\":\"compact blocks\" entries for extended period\n\n#### Root Causes\n1. **Memory exhaustion**: Compaction process runs out of memory (OOM killer)\n2. **I/O saturation**: Disk cannot keep up with compaction reads/writes\n3. **Large cardinality**: Merging blocks with millions of unique series takes too long\n4. **Context canceled**: Compaction cancelled due to shutdown or restart\n5. **File lock contention**: Another process holding file handles\n6. **Index corruption**: Corrupted index file in source block\n\n#### Diagnostic Steps\n\n1. **Check if compaction process exists**:\n   ```bash\n   ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep\n   # Look for CPU/memory usage\n   ```\n\n2. **Monitor compaction duration**:\n   ```promql\n   rate(prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds_sum[5m])\n   / rate(prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds_count[5m])\n   ```\n\n3. **Check for stuck block writes**:\n   ```bash\n   # Look for old `.tmp-for-creation` directories (older than 5 minutes)\n   find /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb -name \"*tmp-for-creation\" \\\n     -type d -mmin +5\n   ```\n\n4. **Check system resources**:\n   ```bash\n   free -h          # Memory availability\n   iostat -x 1 5    # Disk I/O wait times\n   top -b -n 1 | grep prometheus\n   ```\n\n5. **Monitor block metadata**:\n   ```bash\n   # Count total series across blocks\n   for dir in /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/*/meta.json; do\n     grep -o '\"NumSeries\":[0-9]*' \"$dir\"\n   done | awk -F: '{sum+=$2} END {print \"Total series: \" sum}'\n   ```\n\n#### Code References\n- **Compaction loop**: `tsdb/db.go:compactBlocks()` (line 1355-1396)\n- **Block population**: `tsdb/compact.go:DefaultBlockPopulator.PopulateBlock()` (line 729)\n- **Write operation**: `tsdb/compact.go:LeveledCompactor.write()` (line 607-718)\n- **Head compactable check**: `tsdb/head.go:Head.compactable()` (condition for compaction eligibility)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Block Corruption\n\n#### Symptoms\n- `prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total` increases\n- Specific block cannot be loaded: `\"msg\":\"Failed to read meta.json for a block\"`\n- Queries fail when accessing corrupted block time range\n- In logs: `\"corrupted block\"`, `\"failed to read index\"`, or `\"invalid checksum\"` errors\n- Block directory exists but meta.json or index file is unreadable/malformed\n\n#### Root Causes\n1. **Crash during write**: Prometheus crashed mid-compaction → partial block on disk\n2. **Filesystem corruption**: Underlying storage corruption (rare but possible on ext4, XFS issues)\n3. **Stale tmp directories**: Compaction failed and cleanup incomplete\n4. **Meta.json version mismatch**: Invalid metadata structure\n5. **Truncated files**: Out-of-disk-space cut short a write operation\n6. **Index corruption**: Index file overwritten or truncated\n\n#### Diagnostic Steps\n\n1. **Identify corrupted block**:\n   ```bash\n   # Check each block's meta.json\n   for dir in /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/*/; do\n     if ! python3 -m json.tool \"$dir/meta.json\" > /dev/null 2>&1; then\n       echo \"Corrupted: $dir\"\n     fi\n   done\n   ```\n\n2. **Inspect block structure**:\n   ```bash\n   # List expected files in a block\n   ls -la /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/[ULID]/\n   # Should contain: meta.json, index, chunks/, tombstones\n   ```\n\n3. **Check meta.json validity**:\n   ```bash\n   cat /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/[ULID]/meta.json | jq .\n   # Should see valid JSON with `ulid`, `minTime`, `maxTime`, `stats`\n   ```\n\n4. **Verify index file**:\n   ```bash\n   # Index is binary; check file size and header\n   file /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/[ULID]/index\n   ls -lh /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/[ULID]/index\n   ```\n\n5. **Check Prometheus startup logs**:\n   ```bash\n   journalctl -u prometheus -n 100\n   # Look for lines mentioning the block ULID\n   ```\n\n#### Code References\n- **Block loading**: `tsdb/db.go:openBlocks()` (line 1532-1565)\n- **Meta.json parsing**: `tsdb/block.go:readMetaFile()` (reads and validates metadata)\n- **Index opening**: `tsdb/block.go:Block.Index()` (opens index reader)\n- **Corruption detection**: `tsdb/db.go:reloadBlocks()` (line 1440-1478, tracks `corrupted` map)\n- **Repair functions**: `tsdb/repair.go:repairBadIndexVersion()` (historical repair, v2.1)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 4: Out-of-Memory (OOM) During Compaction\n\n#### Symptoms\n- Prometheus process killed by OOM (exit code 137 or \"Killed\" in logs)\n- `dmesg | grep -i \"out of memory\"` shows OOM killer event\n- Compaction never completes; no new blocks created\n- Memory usage spikes during compaction runs\n- In logs: Incomplete compaction metrics + sudden process termination\n\n#### Root Causes\n1. **High cardinality**: Merging blocks with millions of unique series\n2. **Large chunks**: Chunk memory pool exhaustion\n3. **Symbol deduplication**: Merging all label symbols from input blocks\n4. **Index merging**: Postings list merging requires temporary allocations\n5. **Memory limit too low**: Container/system memory limit insufficient for workload\n6. **Memory leak in compaction code**: (Rare) Unreleased memory in merge operations\n\n#### Diagnostic Steps\n\n1. **Monitor memory before compaction**:\n   ```bash\n   # Watch memory during compaction window\n   watch -n 1 'ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep'\n   ```\n\n2. **Check RSS (resident set size)**:\n   ```bash\n   # Get PID and check memory\n   PID=$(pgrep -f \"prometheus.*--storage.tsdb.path\")\n   cat /proc/$PID/status | grep VmRSS\n   ```\n\n3. **Review chunk pool size**:\n   ```bash\n   # Check Prometheus configuration\n   grep -i \"samples-per-chunk\\|chunk\" /etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml\n   # Default: 120 samples per chunk\n   ```\n\n4. **Estimate memory requirement**:\n   ```bash\n   # Approximate formula:\n   # Memory ≈ (# of series) * (avg chunks per series) * (chunk size)\n   # + symbol table + index buffer\n   # For 1M series with 10 chunks, 1KB chunks: ~10GB\n   ```\n\n5. **Check container limits** (if containerized):\n   ```bash\n   # Docker\n   docker inspect <container> | grep -i memory\n\n   # Kubernetes\n   kubectl get pod <prometheus-pod> -o yaml | grep -A 5 resources:\n   ```\n\n#### Code References\n- **Block populator**: `tsdb/compact.go:DefaultBlockPopulator.PopulateBlock()` (line 729, merges all series)\n- **Symbol iteration**: `tsdb/compact.go:PopulateBlock` (line 803-810, merges symbol tables)\n- **Series merging**: `tsdb/compact.go:PopulateBlock` (line 819-870, merges chunk series)\n- **Chunk pool**: `tsdb/chunkenc/pool.go` (memory pooling for chunks)\n- **Head options**: `tsdb/head.go:DefaultHeadOptions()` defines chunk pool sizes\n\n---\n\n## 4. Recovery Procedures\n\n### Recovery 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n#### **Immediate Actions (Before Restart)**\n\n**1. Stop Prometheus gracefully:**\n```bash\nsudo systemctl stop prometheus\n# OR\nkill -SIGTERM $(pgrep -f \"prometheus.*--storage.tsdb.path\")\n# Wait 30 seconds for graceful shutdown\n```\n\n**2. Clean up temporary block directories:**\n```bash\n# SAFE: These are incomplete blocks\nrm -rf /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/*tmp*\ndu -sh /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb\n```\n\n**3. Delete oldest blocks (manual retention):**\n```bash\n# List blocks sorted by creation time\nls -lt /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/ | grep -E '^d'\n\n# Delete oldest blocks until disk usage is acceptable\n# Each block directory name is a ULID; remove by name\nrm -rf /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/[OLDEST_ULID_1]\nrm -rf /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/[OLDEST_ULID_2]\n\n# Verify space\ndu -sh /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb\n```\n\n#### **Configuration Changes (Persistent Fix)**\n\n**4. Adjust retention in Prometheus config (`prometheus.yml`):**\n```yaml\nglobal:\n  # Reduce retention duration (example: 7 days instead of 15)\n  retention:\n    time: 7d\n  # OR set size-based retention\n  retention:\n    size: 50GB\n```\n\n**5. Recalculate block size limits:**\n```bash\n# Formula: MaxBlockDuration = 2 hours (default, in milliseconds)\n# Add to prometheus.yml:\nglobal:\n  storage:\n    tsdb:\n      max-block-duration: 2h    # Compact more frequently\n      min-block-duration: 2h\n      retention:\n        time: 7d\n        size: 50GB  # Hard limit on disk usage\n```\n\n**6. Increase available disk capacity (long-term):**\n```bash\n# Option A: Add storage\ndf -h\n# Add new disk or expand existing partition\nlvextend -L +100G /dev/mapper/vg-lv_prometheus\nresize2fs /dev/mapper/vg-lv_prometheus\n\n# Option B: Archive old blocks to cold storage\ntar czf /archive/prometheus-backup-$(date +%Y%m%d).tar.gz \\\n  /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/[OLDEST_BLOCKS]\nrm -rf /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/[OLDEST_BLOCKS]\n```\n\n#### **Restart and Verify**\n\n**7. Restart Prometheus:**\n```bash\nsudo systemctl start prometheus\nsleep 10\n# Verify startup\nsudo systemctl status prometheus\n```\n\n**8. Verify compaction resumed:**\n```bash\n# Check compaction metrics after 5 minutes\ncurl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query \\\n  'prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total'\n\n# Monitor block cleanup\ncurl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query \\\n  'prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded'\n```\n\n---\n\n### Recovery 2: Compaction Stuck / Not Progressing\n\n#### **Step 1: Verify Stall**\n\n```bash\n# Check compaction rate\ncurl -s 'http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query_range' \\\n  --data-urlencode 'query=rate(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total[5m])' \\\n  --data-urlencode 'start=<5m_ago>' \\\n  --data-urlencode 'end=now' | jq '.data.result'\n\n# If rate is 0 for >10 minutes, compaction is stuck\n```\n\n#### **Step 2: Check System Resources**\n\n```bash\n# Memory\nfree -h\n\n# Disk I/O\niostat -x 1 5\n\n# CPU\ntop -b -n 1 | head -20\n```\n\n#### **Step 3: Inspect Compaction State**\n\n```bash\n# Check for orphaned block writes\nfind /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb -name \"*tmp-for-creation\" -type d\n\n# Check age of tmp directories\nfind /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb -name \"*tmp-for-creation\" \\\n  -type d -exec stat -c '%y %n' {} \\;\n```\n\n#### **Step 4: Graceful Restart (Recommended)**\n\n```bash\n# Stop Prometheus\nsudo systemctl stop prometheus\nsleep 5\n\n# Clean up temp directories\nrm -rf /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/*tmp*\n\n# Check meta.json validity for all blocks\nfor dir in /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/*/; do\n  if ! jq . \"$dir/meta.json\" > /dev/null 2>&1; then\n    echo \"Invalid meta: $dir\"\n  fi\ndone\n\n# Restart\nsudo systemctl start prometheus\n\n# Wait for recovery\nsleep 30\njournalctl -u prometheus -n 50 --no-pager\n```\n\n#### **Step 5: Increase Available Resources (if OOM/Resource-Bound)**\n\n```yaml\n# In prometheus.yml\nglobal:\n  storage:\n    tsdb:\n      # Reduce cardinality during compaction\n      max-block-duration: 1h   # More frequent, smaller compactions\n      min-block-duration: 1h\n      # OR\n      # max-bytes: 20000000000  # Enforce 20GB limit, trigger cleanup\n```\n\n#### **Step 6: Verify Recovery**\n\n```bash\n# Monitor compaction over 10 minutes\nwatch -n 5 'curl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query \\\n  \"prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total\" | jq \".data.result[0].value[1]\"'\n\n# Should increment\n```\n\n---\n\n### Recovery 3: Block Corruption\n\n#### **Step 1: Identify and Isolate Corrupted Block**\n\n```bash\n# Find corrupted blocks\nfor dir in /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/*/; do\n  BLOCK_ID=$(basename \"$dir\")\n  if ! jq . \"$dir/meta.json\" > /dev/null 2>&1; then\n    echo \"CORRUPTED: $BLOCK_ID\"\n  fi\ndone\n```\n\n#### **Step 2: Backup Corrupted Block (Optional)**\n\n```bash\n# Preserve for post-incident analysis\nBLOCK_ID=\"<ULID_of_corrupted_block>\"\ntar czf /backup/prometheus-block-${BLOCK_ID}.tar.gz \\\n  /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/$BLOCK_ID/\n```\n\n#### **Step 3: Delete Corrupted Block**\n\n```bash\n# Remove the corrupted block directory\nrm -rf /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/$BLOCK_ID\n\n# Verify deletion\nls /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/ | grep $BLOCK_ID\n# Should return nothing\n```\n\n#### **Step 4: Restart Prometheus**\n\n```bash\n# Stop and restart to reload block list\nsudo systemctl restart prometheus\nsleep 10\n\n# Monitor reload operation\ncurl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query \\\n  'prometheus_tsdb_reloads_total'\n\n# Check for errors\njournalctl -u prometheus -n 30\n```\n\n#### **Step 5: Verify Data Continuity**\n\n```bash\n# Check time range of loaded blocks\ncurl -s 'http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query' \\\n  --data-urlencode 'query=min(prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded)' | jq\n\n# Query a sample metric to verify blocks are readable\ncurl -s 'http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query' \\\n  --data-urlencode 'query=up' | jq '.data.result | length'\n```\n\n#### **Step 6: Monitor for Data Gap**\n\n```bash\n# Check if queries for the corrupted time range fail gracefully\n# or if adjacent blocks provide data\ncurl -s 'http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query_range' \\\n  --data-urlencode 'query=rate(prometheus_ingestion_samples_total[5m])' \\\n  --data-urlencode 'start=<corrupted_block_start_unix>' \\\n  --data-urlencode 'end=<corrupted_block_end_unix>' | jq\n# Should return empty results or partial results from adjacent blocks\n```\n\n---\n\n### Recovery 4: Out-of-Memory During Compaction\n\n#### **Step 1: Stop Prometheus Immediately**\n\n```bash\n# Kill the process\nsudo systemctl stop prometheus\n# OR\nkill -9 $(pgrep -f \"prometheus.*--storage.tsdb.path\")\n\n# Wait for process to fully terminate\nsleep 5\nps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep  # Verify killed\n```\n\n#### **Step 2: Reduce Workload / Cardinality**\n\n```bash\n# Option A: Reduce scrape targets\n# Edit prometheus.yml and comment out high-cardinality scrape_configs\nsudo vi /etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml\n\n# Option B: Reduce samples per chunk (lower memory per block)\n# Add to global section:\nglobal:\n  storage:\n    tsdb:\n      samples-per-chunk: 60  # Default 120; reduces memory footprint\n```\n\n#### **Step 3: Check Block Layout**\n\n```bash\n# Count current blocks and estimate memory requirement\nTOTAL_SERIES=$(for dir in /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/*/meta.json; do\n  grep -o '\"NumSeries\":[0-9]*' \"$dir\"\ndone | awk -F: '{sum+=$2} END {print sum}')\n\nTOTAL_CHUNKS=$(for dir in /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/*/meta.json; do\n  grep -o '\"NumChunks\":[0-9]*' \"$dir\"\ndone | awk -F: '{sum+=$2} END {print sum}')\n\necho \"Total Series: $TOTAL_SERIES\"\necho \"Total Chunks: $TOTAL_CHUNKS\"\necho \"Estimated Peak Memory During Compaction: ~$((TOTAL_CHUNKS / 100))MB (rough)\"\n```\n\n#### **Step 4: Increase System Memory (if Possible)**\n\n```bash\n# Container-based (Docker)\ndocker update --memory 4g <container_name>\n\n# Kubernetes (edit YAML)\nkubectl edit pod <prometheus-pod>\n# Update resources.limits.memory and resources.requests.memory\n\n# VM-based (if possible, increase available RAM)\n# Add swap as temporary measure (not recommended long-term)\nsudo fallocate -l 2G /swapfile\nsudo chmod 600 /swapfile\nsudo mkswap /swapfile\nsudo swapon /swapfile\n```\n\n#### **Step 5: Enforce More Frequent, Smaller Compactions**\n\n```yaml\n# In prometheus.yml\nglobal:\n  storage:\n    tsdb:\n      # Compact more frequently with smaller blocks\n symbol table (~1-10% overhead)\nESTIMATED_MB=$(( (NUM_SAMPLES * 8) / 1000000 ))\necho \"Estimated peak memory during compaction: ~${ESTIMATED_MB}MB\"\n```\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nPrometheus TSDB compaction is a critical background process that:\n- Merges overlapping blocks for consistency and query speed\n- Removes deleted series to recover disk space\n- Is triggered automatically every minute and on-demand after head commits\n- Must be monitored for stalls, failures, and resource exhaustion\n\nKey recovery strategies:\n1. **Disk exhaustion**: Delete old blocks, adjust retention\n2. **Stuck compaction**: Restart, clean tmp dirs, add resources\n3. **Block corruption**: Delete corrupted block, reload blocks\n4. **OOM**: Restart, reduce workload, increase memory, adjust block duration\n\nRegular monitoring of `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total`, `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total`, and `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` enables early detection of compaction Overview\n\n### What Compaction Does\n\nCompaction in Prometheus TSDB merges multiple time-series data blocks into larger, more efficient blocks. This process:\n\n- **Merges overlapping blocks**: Combines blocks with overlapping time ranges into a single block to improve query performance and consistency\n- **Removes deleted series**: Eliminates tombstoned (deleted) series from blocks, reducing disk space usage\n- **Deduplicates samples**: Consolidates duplicate samples from overlapping blocks\n- **Optimizes index and chunk layout**: Reorganizes data for better I/O efficiency and memory locality\n\n### Compaction Levels and Block Structure\n\nPrometheus uses **exponential compaction levels**:\n\n- **Level 1**: Freshly persisted head blocks (2-hour default duration)\n- **Level 2**: First-level compaction (4-hour range)\n- **Level 3**: Second-level compaction (8-hour range)\n- **Level N**: Progressive doubling of time ranges\n\nEach level is defined by:\n- **MinTime (mint)**: Start timestamp (milliseconds, inclusive)\n- **MaxTime (maxt)**: End timestamp (milliseconds, exclusive)\n- **ULID**: Unique identifier for the block\n- **Compaction.Level**: Current compaction level\n- **Compaction.Parents**: Source blocks that were compacted\n- **Compaction.Sources**: Original blocks the compact traces back to\n\n### When Compaction is Triggered\n\nCompaction is triggered by three mechanisms:\n\n#### 1. Time-Based Triggering (Primary)\n- A background goroutine runs every **1 minute** (line 995 in db.go)\n- Checks if the head block is **compactable** (time window has passed)\n- Sends trigger signal to `compactc` channel\n\n#### 2. Appender-Based Triggering (On-Demand)\n- After each commit to the head block, checks `head.compactable()` (line 1120 in db.go)\n- If compactable, immediately triggers compaction without waiting for the 1-minute interval\n- Ensures fresh data is persisted promptly\n\n#### 3. Retention-Based Triggering (Post-Compaction)\n- After block compaction succeeds, `reloadBlocks()` checks for:\n  - **Time retention**: Blocks older than `RetentionDuration` are marked deletable\n  - **Size retention**: If `MaxBytes` is set, oldest blocks are removed until total size <= `MaxBytes`\n- Compaction plan considers blocks with **>5% tombstones** for cleanup (line 281 in compact.go)\n\n### Compaction Flow\n\n```\nHead Block Data (2h window)\n    ↓ (compactable after 1h min wait)\nHead Compaction → Level 1 Block\n    ↓ (time-based plan check)\nCompactor.Plan() → identifies compactable blocks\n    ↓\nCompactor.Compact() → merges blocks, removes tombstones\n    ↓\nDB.reloadBlocks() → swaps in new block, deletes parents\n    ↓\nRetention cleanup → removes old/oversized blocks\n```\n\n---\n\n## 2. Monitoring Indicators\n\n### Key Prometheus Metrics\n\n#### Compaction Activity Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Meaning | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|---------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` | Counter | Total compactions executed | Track for stalls (no increase for >10 min) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total` | Counter | Total compactions triggered | Should increase ~every 1 min |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` | Counter | Failed compactions | Alert if > 0 |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total` | Counter | Overlapping block compactions | Indicates overlapping blocks detected |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` | Histogram | Compaction wall-clock time | P95 > 5 min = slow compaction |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` | Gauge | 1 if block being written | Should be 0 for >30 sec (stuck write) |\n\n#### Block Management Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Meaning | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|---------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` | Gauge | Currently loaded blocks | Rapid increases = blocks not cleaning up |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes_total` | Gauge | Total block disk usage | Should trend toward `MaxBytes` limit |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_reloads_total` | Counter | Block reload operations | Once per minute (normal) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total` | Counter | Failed block reloads | Alert if > 0 |\n\n#### Chunk Compaction Metrics (Level 1 Only)\n\n| Metric | Type | Meaning | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|---------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_size_bytes` | Histogram | Final chunk sizes | Very small (<100 B) or large (>50 KB) chunks indicate compression issues |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_samples` | Histogram | Samples per chunk | <50 or >1000 samples per chunk = efficiency loss |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_range_seconds` | Histogram | Time span of chunks | Anomalies indicate data collection issues |\n\n### Alert Rules\n\n#### Critical Alerts (Act Immediately)\n\n```promql\n# Compaction is failing\nrate(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total[5m]) > 0\n\n# Block reload failures\nrate(prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total[5m]) > 0\n\n# Disk space about to be exhausted (if MaxBytes set)\nprometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes_total\n  / prometheus_tsdb_max_bytes_limit\n  > 0.95\n```\n\n#### Warning Alerts (Investigate Within 1 Hour)\n\n```promql\n# Compaction is stuck/slow\nrate(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total[10m]) == 0\n\n# Compaction taking too long\nhistogram_quantile(0.95,\n  prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds_bucket) > 300\n\n# Block populating stalled\nprometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block == 1\n  and time() - timestamp(prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block) > 30\n```\n\n### Healthy Compaction Patterns\n\n- **Compactions triggered**: ~1 per minute (every minute the goroutine checks)\n- **Compactions executed**: ~1 per 5-30 minutes (depends on block layout and activity)\n- **Compaction duration**: P50 < 1s, P99 < 5s (for typical setups)\n- **Blocks loaded**: Stable count (typically 10-50 for normal retention)\n- **Reload failures**: Zero\n- **Block bytes**: Trending toward configured limit\n\n---\n\n## 3. Failure Modes\n\n### Failure Mode 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n#### Symptoms\n- Compaction fails with \"no space left on device\" error\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` increases\n- New blocks cannot be persisted to disk\n- Ingestion slows or stops\n- In logs: `\"msg\":\"compact ... : no such file or directory\"` or similar I/O errors\n\n#### Root Causes\n1. **Retention duration too long**: `RetentionDuration` retains data beyond disk capacity\n2. **MaxBytes limit not enforced**: `MaxBytes` set but blocks not deleting fast enough\n3. **Compaction blocked**: Compaction unable to run → old blocks accumulate\n4. **Unexpected large metrics**: Cardinality explosion or high-frequency scraping\n5. **WAL growth**: Write-ahead log (WAL) consuming large disk space\n6. **Tmp block directories not cleaned**: Failed compactions leave `.tmp-for-creation` directories\n\n#### Diagnostic Steps\n\n1. **Check disk usage**:\n   ```bash\n   df -h /path/to/prometheus/data\n   du -sh /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb\n   du -sh /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/wal\n   ```\n\n2. **Inspect block count and size**:\n   ```bash\n   ls -lh /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/ | grep -E '^d' | wc -l\n   find /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb -name \"meta.json\" | wc -l\n   ```\n\n3. **Check for tmp directories**:\n   ```bash\n   find /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb -name \"*tmp*\" -type d\n   ```\n\n4. **Monitor compaction metrics**:\n   ```promql\n   rate(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total[5m])\n   prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes_total\n   ```\n\n5. **Check Prometheus logs for errors**:\n   ```bash\n   grep -i \"disk\\|space\\|compaction\\|failed\" /var/log/prometheus/*.log | tail -50\n   ```\n\n#### Code References\n- **Compaction triggering**: `tsdb/db.go:run()` (line 982-1027)\n- **Retention cleanup**: `tsdb/db.go:DefaultBlocksToDelete()` (defines retention policy)\n- **Compaction execution**: `tsdb/compact.go:LeveledCompactor.Compact()` (line 444)\n- **Disk space checks**: `tsdb/db.go:reloadBlocks()` (line 1424-1530)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 2: Compaction Stuck / Not Progressing\n\n#### Symptoms\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` metric flat (no increment for 10+ minutes)\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` gauge stuck at 1\n- Memory usage climbing or stable at high level\n- Queries slow (many blocks to search)\n- In logs: No \"msg\":\"compact blocks\" entries for extended period\n\n#### Root Causes\n1. **Memory exhaustion**: Compaction process runs out of memory (OOM killer)\n2. **I/O saturation**: Disk cannot keep up with compaction reads/writes\n3. **Large cardinality**: Merging blocks with millions of unique series takes too long\n4. **Context canceled**: Compaction cancelled due to shutdown or restart\n5. **File lock contention**: Another process holding file handles\n6. **Index corruption**: Corrupted index file in source block\n\n#### Diagnostic Steps\n\n1. **Check if compaction process exists**:\n   ```bash\n   ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep\n   # Look for CPU/memory usage\n   ```\n\n2. **Monitor compaction duration**:\n   ```promql\n   rate(prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds_sum[5m])\n   / rate(prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds_count[5m])\n   ```\n\n3. **Check for stuck block writes**:\n   ```bash\n   # Look for old `.tmp-for-creation` directories (older than 5 minutes)\n   find /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb -name \"*tmp-for-creation\" \\\n     -type d -mmin +5\n   ```\n\n4. **Check system resources**:\n   ```bash\n   free -h          # Memory availability\n   iostat -x 1 5    # Disk I/O wait times\n   top -b -n 1 | grep prometheus\n   ```\n\n5. **Monitor block metadata**:\n   ```bash\n   # Count total series across blocks\n   for dir in /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/*/meta.json; do\n     grep -o '\"NumSeries\":[0-9]*' \"$dir\"\n   done | awk -F: '{sum+=$2} END {print \"Total series: \" sum}'\n   ```\n\n#### Code References\n- **Compaction loop**: `tsdb/db.go:compactBlocks()` (line 1355-1396)\n- **Block population**: `tsdb/compact.go:DefaultBlockPopulator.PopulateBlock()` (line 729)\n- **Write operation**: `tsdb/compact.go:LeveledCompactor.write()` (line 607-718)\n- **Head compactable check**: `tsdb/head.go:Head.compactable()` (condition for compaction eligibility)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Block Corruption\n\n#### Symptoms\n- `prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total` increases\n- Specific block cannot be loaded: `\"msg\":\"Failed to read meta.json for a block\"`\n- Queries fail when accessing corrupted block time range\n- In logs: `\"corrupted block\"`, `\"failed to read index\"`, or `\"invalid checksum\"` errors\n- Block directory exists but meta.json or index file is unreadable/malformed\n\n#### Root Causes\n1. **Crash during write**: Prometheus crashed mid-compaction → partial block on disk\n2. **Filesystem corruption**: Underlying storage corruption (rare but possible on ext4, XFS issues)\n3. **Stale tmp directories**: Compaction failed and cleanup incomplete\n4. **Meta.json version mismatch**: Invalid metadata structure\n5. **Truncated files**: Out-of-disk-space cut short a write operation\n6. **Index corruption**: Index file overwritten or truncated\n\n#### Diagnostic Steps\n\n1. **Identify corrupted block**:\n   ```bash\n   # Check each block's meta.json\n   for dir in /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/*/; do\n     if ! python3 -m json.tool \"$dir/meta.json\" > /dev/null 2>&1; then\n       echo \"Corrupted: $dir\"\n     fi\n   done\n   ```\n\n2. **Inspect block structure**:\n   ```bash\n   # List expected files in a block\n   ls -la /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/[ULID]/\n   # Should contain: meta.json, index, chunks/, tombstones\n   ```\n\n3. **Check meta.json validity**:\n   ```bash\n   cat /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/[ULID]/meta.json | jq .\n   # Should see valid JSON with `ulid`, `minTime`, `maxTime`, `stats`\n   ```\n\n4. **Verify index file**:\n   ```bash\n   # Index is binary; check file size and header\n   file /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/[ULID]/index\n   ls -lh /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/[ULID]/index\n   ```\n\n5. **Check Prometheus startup logs**:\n   ```bash\n   journalctl -u prometheus -n 100\n   # Look for lines mentioning the block ULID\n   ```\n\n#### Code References\n- **Block loading**: `tsdb/db.go:openBlocks()` (line 1532-1565)\n- **Meta.json parsing**: `tsdb/block.go:readMetaFile()` (reads and validates metadata)\n- **Index opening**: `tsdb/block.go:Block.Index()` (opens index reader)\n- **Corruption detection**: `tsdb/db.go:reloadBlocks()` (line 1440-1478, tracks `corrupted` map)\n- **Repair functions**: `tsdb/repair.go:repairBadIndexVersion()` (historical repair, v2.1)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 4: Out-of-Memory (OOM) During Compaction\n\n#### Symptoms\n- Prometheus process killed by OOM (exit code 137 or \"Killed\" in logs)\n- `dmesg | grep -i \"out of memory\"` shows OOM killer event\n- Compaction never completes; no new blocks created\n- Memory usage spikes during compaction runs\n- In logs: Incomplete compaction metrics + sudden process termination\n\n#### Root Causes\n1. **High cardinality**: Merging blocks with millions of unique series\n2. **Large chunks**: Chunk memory pool exhaustion\n3. **Symbol deduplication**: Merging all label symbols from input blocks\n4. **Index merging**: Postings list merging requires temporary allocations\n5. **Memory limit too low**: Container/system memory limit insufficient for workload\n6. **Memory leak in compaction code**: (Rare) Unreleased memory in merge operations\n\n#### Diagnostic Steps\n\n1. **Monitor memory before compaction**:\n   ```bash\n   # Watch memory during compaction window\n   watch -n 1 'ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep'\n   ```\n\n2. **Check RSS (resident set size)**:\n   ```bash\n   # Get PID and check memory\n   PID=$(pgrep -f \"prometheus.*--storage.tsdb.path\")\n   cat /proc/$PID/status | grep VmRSS\n   ```\n\n3. **Review chunk pool size**:\n   ```bash\n   # Check Prometheus configuration\n   grep -i \"samples-per-chunk\\|chunk\" /etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml\n   # Default: 120 samples per chunk\n   ```\n\n4. **Estimate memory requirement**:\n   ```bash\n   # Approximate formula:\n   # Memory ≈ (# of series) * (avg chunks per series) * (chunk size)\n   # + symbol table + index buffer\n   # For 1M series with 10 chunks, 1KB chunks: ~10GB\n   ```\n\n5. **Check container limits** (if containerized):\n   ```bash\n   # Docker\n   docker inspect <container> | grep -i memory\n\n   # Kubernetes\n   kubectl get pod <prometheus-pod> -o yaml | grep -A 5 resources:\n   ```\n\n#### Code References\n- **Block populator**: `tsdb/compact.go:DefaultBlockPopulator.PopulateBlock()` (line 729, merges all series)\n- **Symbol iteration**: `tsdb/compact.go:PopulateBlock` (line 803-810, merges symbol tables)\n- **Series merging**: `tsdb/compact.go:PopulateBlock` (line 819-870, merges chunk series)\n- **Chunk pool**: `tsdb/chunkenc/pool.go` (memory pooling for chunks)\n- **Head options**: `tsdb/head.go:DefaultHeadOptions()` defines chunk pool sizes\n\n---\n\n## 4. Recovery Procedures\n\n### Recovery 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n#### **Immediate Actions (Before Restart)**\n\n**1. Stop Prometheus gracefully:**\n```bash\nsudo systemctl stop prometheus\n# OR\nkill -SIGTERM $(pgrep -f \"prometheus.*--storage.tsdb.path\")\n# Wait 30 seconds for graceful shutdown\n```\n\n**2. Clean up temporary block directories:**\n```bash\n# SAFE: These are incomplete blocks\nrm -rf /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/*tmp*\ndu -sh /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb\n```\n\n**3. Delete oldest blocks (manual retention):**\n```bash\n# List blocks sorted by creation time\nls -lt /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/ | grep -E '^d'\n\n# Delete oldest blocks until disk usage is acceptable\n# Each block directory name is a ULID; remove by name\nrm -rf /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/[OLDEST_ULID_1]\nrm -rf /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/[OLDEST_ULID_2]\n\n# Verify space\ndu -sh /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb\n```\n\n#### **Configuration Changes (Persistent Fix)**\n\n**4. Adjust retention in Prometheus config (`prometheus.yml`):**\n```yaml\nglobal:\n  # Reduce retention duration (example: 7 days instead of 15)\n  retention:\n    time: 7d\n  # OR set size-based retention\n  retention:\n    size: 50GB\n```\n\n**5. Recalculate block size limits:**\n```bash\n# Formula: MaxBlockDuration = 2 hours (default, in milliseconds)\n# Add to prometheus.yml:\nglobal:\n  storage:\n    tsdb:\n      max-block-duration: 2h    # Compact more frequently\n      min-block-duration: 2h\n      retention:\n        time: 7d\n        size: 50GB  # Hard limit on disk usage\n```\n\n**6. Increase available disk capacity (long-term):**\n```bash\n# Option A: Add storage\ndf -h\n# Add new disk or expand existing partition\nlvextend -L +100G /dev/mapper/vg-lv_prometheus\nresize2fs /dev/mapper/vg-lv_prometheus\n\n# Option B: Archive old blocks to cold storage\ntar czf /archive/prometheus-backup-$(date +%Y%m%d).tar.gz \\\n  /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/[OLDEST_BLOCKS]\nrm -rf /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/[OLDEST_BLOCKS]\n```\n\n#### **Restart and Verify**\n\n**7. Restart Prometheus:**\n```bash\nsudo systemctl start prometheus\nsleep 10\n# Verify startup\nsudo systemctl status prometheus\n```\n\n**8. Verify compaction resumed:**\n```bash\n# Check compaction metrics after 5 minutes\ncurl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query \\\n  'prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total'\n\n# Monitor block cleanup\ncurl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query \\\n  'prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded'\n```\n\n---\n\n### Recovery 2: Compaction Stuck / Not Progressing\n\n#### **Step 1: Verify Stall**\n\n```bash\n# Check compaction rate\ncurl -s 'http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query_range' \\\n  --data-urlencode 'query=rate(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total[5m])' \\\n  --data-urlencode 'start=<5m_ago>' \\\n  --data-urlencode 'end=now' | jq '.data.result'\n\n# If rate is 0 for >10 minutes, compaction is stuck\n```\n\n#### **Step 2: Check System Resources**\n\n```bash\n# Memory\nfree -h\n\n# Disk I/O\niostat -x 1 5\n\n# CPU\ntop -b -n 1 | head -20\n```\n\n#### **Step 3: Inspect Compaction State**\n\n```bash\n# Check for orphaned block writes\nfind /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb -name \"*tmp-for-creation\" -type d\n\n# Check age of tmp directories\nfind /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb -name \"*tmp-for-creation\" \\\n  -type d -exec stat -c '%y %n' {} \\;\n```\n\n#### **Step 4: Graceful Restart (Recommended)**\n\n```bash\n# Stop Prometheus\nsudo systemctl stop prometheus\nsleep 5\n\n# Clean up temp directories\nrm -rf /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/*tmp*\n\n# Check meta.json validity for all blocks\nfor dir in /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/*/; do\n  if ! jq . \"$dir/meta.json\" > /dev/null 2>&1; then\n    echo \"Invalid meta: $dir\"\n  fi\ndone\n\n# Restart\nsudo systemctl start prometheus\n\n# Wait for recovery\nsleep 30\njournalctl -u prometheus -n 50 --no-pager\n```\n\n#### **Step 5: Increase Available Resources (if OOM/Resource-Bound)**\n\n```yaml\n# In prometheus.yml\nglobal:\n  storage:\n    tsdb:\n      # Reduce cardinality during compaction\n      max-block-duration: 1h   # More frequent, smaller compactions\n      min-block-duration: 1h\n      # OR\n      # max-bytes: 20000000000  # Enforce 20GB limit, trigger cleanup\n```\n\n#### **Step 6: Verify Recovery**\n\n```bash\n# Monitor compaction over 10 minutes\nwatch -n 5 'curl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query \\\n  \"prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total\" | jq \".data.result[0].value[1]\"'\n\n# Should increment\n```\n\n---\n\n### Recovery 3: Block Corruption\n\n#### **Step 1: Identify and Isolate Corrupted Block**\n\n```bash\n# Find corrupted blocks\nfor dir in /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/*/; do\n  BLOCK_ID=$(basename \"$dir\")\n  if ! jq . \"$dir/meta.json\" > /dev/null 2>&1; then\n    echo \"CORRUPTED: $BLOCK_ID\"\n  fi\ndone\n```\n\n#### **Step 2: Backup Corrupted Block (Optional)**\n\n```bash\n# Preserve for post-incident analysis\nBLOCK_ID=\"<ULID_of_corrupted_block>\"\ntar czf /backup/prometheus-block-${BLOCK_ID}.tar.gz \\\n  /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/$BLOCK_ID/\n```\n\n#### **Step 3: Delete Corrupted Block**\n\n```bash\n# Remove the corrupted block directory\nrm -rf /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/$BLOCK_ID\n\n# Verify deletion\nls /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/ | grep $BLOCK_ID\n# Should return nothing\n```\n\n#### **Step 4: Restart Prometheus**\n\n```bash\n# Stop and restart to reload block list\nsudo systemctl restart prometheus\nsleep 10\n\n# Monitor reload operation\ncurl -s the corrupted time range fail gracefully\n# or if adjacent blocks provide data\ncurl -s 'http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query_range' \\\n  --data-urlencode results or partial results from adjacent blocks\n```\n\n---\n\n### Recovery 4: Out-of-Memory During Compaction\n\n#### **Step 1: Stop Prometheus Immediately**\n\n```bash\n# Kill the process\nsudo /etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml\n\n# Option B: Reduce samples per chunk (lower memory per block)\n# Add to global section:\nglobal:\n  storage:\n    tsdb:\n      samples-per-chunk: 60  # Default 120; reduces memory footprint\n```\n\n#### **Step 3: Check Block Layout**\n\n```bash\n# Count current blocks and estimate memory requirement\nTOTAL_SERIES=$(for dir in /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/*/meta.json; do\n  grep -o '\"NumSeries\":[0-9]*' \"$dir\"\ndone | awk -F: '{sum+=$2} END {print sum}')\n\nTOTAL_CHUNKS=$(for dir in /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/*/meta.json; do\n  grep -o '\"NumChunks\":[0-9]*' \"$dir\"\ndone | awk -F: '{sum+=$2} END {print sum}')\n\necho \"Total Series: $TOTAL_SERIES\"\necho \"Total Chunks: $TOTAL_CHUNKS\"\necho \"Estimated Peak Memory During Compaction: ~$((TOTAL_CHUNKS / 100))MB (rough)\"\n```\n\n#### **Step 4: Increase System Memory (if Possible)**\n\n```bash\n# Container-based (Docker)\ndocker update --memory 4g <container_name>\n\n# Kubernetes (edit YAML)\nkubectl edit pod <prometheus-pod>\n# Update resources.limits.memory and resources.requests.memory\n\n# VM-based (if /swapfile\n```\n\n#### **Step 5: Enforce More Frequent, Smaller Compactions**\n\n```yaml\n# In prometheus.yml\nglobal:\n  storage:\n    tsdb:\n      # Compact more frequently with smaller blocks\n
